Important News

American Professor Reveals Japanese Conspiracy 74

Japan Considers the US its Primary Enemy, Followed by Russia

Seizing Manchuria with the Japan-France Agreement as Backup

The Nagasaki Nichinichi Shimbun published a lengthy article on the 18th entitled [American Views on Japan]. The article provides insight into the psychology of the Japanese and American peoples. A translation is provided below. Recently, the Hearst newspapers in the United States have often made statements expressing fear of Japan. However, the malicious words and wanton attacks on Japan by these newspapers are not surprising. However, the fact that a certain individual who has resided in Japan for seven years, is familiar with the situation in Japan, and is a professor at a Japanese high school has also made such statements is indeed worthy of our attention. His words are: We should know the situation in Japan today and the psychology of the Japanese towards the United States. The negative feelings of the Japanese towards the United States are deeply ingrained, and the reason for this is that after President Roosevelt acted as a mediator at the end of the Russo-Japanese War, Japan could not seize Manchuria and could not obtain compensation from Russia. As a result, it only obtained the southern half of Sakhalin Island. This was the beginning of the Japanese hating the United States. After that, the passage of anti-Japanese laws in California, opposition to the Twenty-One Demands, and other events followed one after another. During the European War, the United States prevented Japan's Siberian expedition from advancing east of Lake Baikal. Last year, the Manchurian Incident suddenly broke out, and the United States intervened again. As a result, Japan was repeatedly constrained by the United States and could not achieve what it wanted. The Japanese have long known that a war between Japan and the United States is difficult to avoid, but it is only a matter of time. Since the enactment of the Asian Exclusion Act in 1923, the Japanese Navy has been preparing for battle. At that time, Japan's will to fight was extremely strong, but the Great Kanto Earthquake occurred, and the idea of fighting disappeared. After the Manchurian Incident broke out this time, the United States did not change its long-standing policy and interfered. As a result, the image of the United States in the minds of the Japanese became increasingly recognized as an obstructer, a hypocritical gentleman, a cold-blooded man (as before, when the United States excluded the Asian race, Japan condemned the United States as a hypocritical gentleman, prevented Japan's inevitable territorial expansion, and condemned the United States as a cold-blooded man, and in all other actions of the United States against Japan, it was always made difficult). However, the proponents of war in Japan were not only the military, but also the entire pro-war nation. These pro-war citizens incited the military to go to war with the United States. For example, in Osaka, the wife of an officer committed suicide to persuade her husband to cut off his concerns so that her husband could serve the country wholeheartedly. This kind of fact is carried out among the people and praised by the government and army officers. Therefore, Japan believes that with this indomitable spirit, martial spirit, and national unity, it can be assured of victory in a war with the United States. It has also said that Japan's naval power is quite dominant among the countries of the world today. Holding such an exaggerated idea to confront the United States, it usually refers to the United States as its primary enemy, followed by Russia. However, although Japan boasts that it can be assured of victory, what it fears is the US Air Force. Therefore, recently, major Japanese cities have been urgently practicing air warfare. However, Japan's aviation technology is quite immature, and Japan also knows that it is not a match for the United States. Therefore, at the recent Geneva Disarmament Conference, it proposed the abolition of aircraft carriers. At that time, when we heard that Japan was proposing this plan, we could not help but laugh, because its fear had been publicly exposed. The outbreak of the September 18th Incident last year was caused by the Japanese military itself destroying the South Manchuria Railway. This has already been mentioned in the Tanaka Memorial. As far as we are concerned, although the Japanese government officially denies it, its ambition to conquer the world is undoubtedly clear. The invasion of Manchuria is a prerequisite for realizing its ambition. After Manchuria is obtained, it can obtain endless resources such as gold, coal, and forests. Not only can it surpass the United States, but it can also increase its wealth by more than three times. What is most noteworthy among them is the Japan-France secret agreement. This agreement was concluded after the abolition of the Anglo-Japanese Alliance. France allowed Japan to send troops to Siberia and recognized its seizure of the land east of Lake Baikal. The reason why Japan dared to seize Manchuria was that it had this agreement as its backing. Therefore, France is nothing less than a Japanese lantern leader. This view is also known to all countries in the world, so there is no need to avoid it. (The following is omitted)

Recent Political Situation in North China 75

Zhang Xueliang Has Cancelled His Intention to Go Abroad

Yu Xuezhong is Scheduled to Arrive in Tianjin Next Week to Take Office

Internal Unity, Local Security as Usual

Tianjin Correspondence: Since President Wang Jingwei submitted his resignation to the Central Government, Zhang Xueliang, Director of the Peiping Pacification Headquarters, had no choice but to resolutely resign due to environmental reasons, so as to avoid being criticized by all parties. Although more than 50 generals in North China, such as Song Zheyuan, Wan Fulin, Yu Xuezhong, Wang Shuchang, and Tang Yulin, jointly telegraphed the day before yesterday, stating that they would advance and retreat with Zhang, the actual situation is not serious. The generals have followed Zhang's father and son for many years and have been through thick and thin together. On weekdays, Zhang's subordinates are also very harmonious in terms of feelings. This time, Zhang's departure must be expressed in order to comfort Zhang's heart. This is one reason. Furthermore, the generals in North China, witnessing the three northeastern provinces being seized by the violent Japanese and unable to recover the lost territory, should also understand the overall situation, unite internally, and wait for the day to plan a permanent anti-Japanese plan. They definitely do not want to cause unrest in the political situation in North China due to Zhang's personal resignation. This is the second reason. With these two reasons, after the telegram was issued, once Zhang personally comforted and exhorted the generals separately, urging them not to have any excessive remarks, it would be safe and sound. As for whether Zhang will go abroad or stay in Peiping to continue to be responsible for military and political affairs in North China, the reporter was told by Provincial Chairman Wang Shuchang yesterday that it has not yet been decided. However, according to general speculation, there are many problems hindering Zhang's going abroad, so it seems more likely that he will stay in Peiping, or he may still serve as the chairman of the Military Affairs Committee branch. It is also unknown. Because of Zhang Xueliang's resignation, the issue of the change of chairman of Hebei Province has been triggered. This has been decided by the northern authorities and telegraphed to the National Government for appointment. The National Government has now issued an order transferring Yu Xuezhong to be the chairman of Hebei Province, and Wang Shuchang to be the commander of the Peiping-Tianjin Garrison. The military positions held by Yu and Wang will remain the same. After Chairman Wang returned to Tianjin from Peiping yesterday, he immediately instructed the departments to handle the handover matters, and convened his subordinates to give a speech in the provincial government, the general idea being that everyone should not lose heart because of his personal departure, and should still assist the new Chairman Yu in handling affairs with the same spirit as before. As for the department heads and provincial committee members under the jurisdiction of the provincial government, there was also news of a general resignation the day before yesterday due to Chairman Wang's transfer, but after Wang's persuasion yesterday, the intention of general resignation has been cancelled. However, the positions of the heads of the finance and civil affairs departments are important, and it has been widely reported here that they will be replaced. The most promising candidate for the head of finance is Zhang Zhenlu, the former head of the Liaoning Finance Department. Although the position of the head of civil affairs is rumored to be unstable, there is still some chance of being reappointed. Mayor Zhou Longguang is still suitable for dealing with Japanese diplomacy, and is expected to continue in office based on the current situation. According to this political development, local security has not been affected in the slightest. This is also because the military and political authorities are well aware of the overall situation and do not want to give the Japanese an opportunity to take advantage of. It is heard that the new chairman, Yu Xuezhong, has decided to come to Tianjin to take office next Tuesday or Wednesday. (20th)

Expanding Air Force in Guizhou and Guangdong 76

Guizhou Aviation Bureau Hires American-Trained Pilots as Instructors

Guangdong Continues Promoting Aviation Bonds for New Fighters

Guangzhou Report: The provinces of Guizhou and Guangdong have recently been making great efforts to expand their air forces. In Guizhou, after Bai Chongxi and Li Zongren returned to Guizhou the year before last, they immediately set their minds to establishing an aviation bureau to build up air power. However, at that time, Guizhou lacked aviation talent and had to borrow personnel from Guangdong. When Li Zongren came to Guangzhou to participate in the Southwest National Government, he discussed with the Guangdong Air Force Headquarters about allocating a group of flight personnel to Guizhou to establish an aviation bureau. Zhang Huichang then sent Ao Yuanqing, He Jingwei, Liang Qingquan, Yu Bingyang, Huang Yihe, Deng Xianggang, Yuan Jiaqi, Chen Qiguang, Li Lingyun, Zhou Yiping, Zhang Jian, Huang Fengming, Liu Guoquan, Huang Yuanbo, and more than a dozen others to serve in the Guizhou Aviation Bureau. Lin Weicheng, the former advisor to the Fourth Group Army of Guizhou Province (also from the Guangdong Air Force and formerly the Director of the Guangdong Aviation Bureau), was appointed as the Deputy Director. The bureau's internal organization was divided into a training section, with chief and deputy flight instructors, chief and deputy mechanical instructors, a chief mechanic, senior and junior instructors, all of whom were assigned to the above-mentioned personnel. Since its establishment in Nanning, the bureau has graduated aviation and mechanical classes, each with thirty students. Unexpectedly, the Guizhou authorities, for some reason, suddenly dismissed all the aviation officers who had been introduced by Zhang Huichang of Guangdong to serve in Guizhou this month, paying them half a month's salary and sending them away. This group of Guangdong pilots returned to Guangdong on the 9th. After the dismissal of these personnel, it is rumored that Deng Yueming and Yang Guanyu, who had previously been dismissed from their posts in Guangdong and were staying in Hong Kong, would be hired to serve in Guizhou. However, this has not yet been implemented. If the Guizhou Bureau had not dismissed the Guizhou Aviation Bureau personnel due to political reasons, there would have been no reason to recruit Deng and Yang, who were close to Zhang Huichang, from Hong Kong. Now, considering that Li Zongren has recently hired American-trained aviation personnel returning from the United States to Guizhou, it is possible that the dismissal of all personnel from the Guizhou Aviation Bureau had a political purpose. It is reported that the three American students recently hired by Li Zongren in Hong Kong, Zhang Haoyuan, Wang Demin, and Wu Yaosong, were hired to go to Nanning to serve as flight instructors in the Aviation Bureau. As for the Guangdong Aviation Department, since Zhang Huichang's faction lost power, Huang Guangrui is now reorganizing everything. Recently, there has been news of the expansion of one more squadron. There were only five squadrons, and now it is planned to form a sixth squadron. During Zhang Huichang's tenure, he purchased a batch of fighter planes from a certain country. After Zhang's departure, the purchase contract was taken away by Zhang, so when the planes arrived in Hong Kong, Zhang and the Guangdong government argued over who would take delivery. The Guangdong government had the funds but not the contract, while Zhang held the contract but lacked the funds to take delivery. The two sides were in a long legal battle. Guangdong sent Zhu Zhaoxin to Hong Kong to negotiate using diplomatic means and prepared a large sum of money to purchase the planes. As a result, Zhang Huichang's side failed, and the planes that were shipped were taken over by the Guangdong government. They arrived in Guangzhou yesterday. It is said that these planes are new [Douglas] fighter planes, with machine guns placed in the front, back, left, and right, and a very high flight speed. Five planes have already arrived and have been received by the Air Force Headquarters. The Air Force Headquarters yesterday appointed Hu Jinya (the former commander of the First Aircraft Squadron), who had just returned from the United States to raise funds, as the Air Force Chief of Staff. Hu took office yesterday, the 15th. The government advocates continuing to promote the aviation bonds previously issued by the Air Force to purchase more planes. Chen Jitang has ordered that 3 million be sold within a limited time, with 1.5 million to be sold in Guangzhou and the remaining 1.5 million to be sold in various counties and cities throughout Guangdong Province, with specific sales quotas. Shantou, Nanhai, and Zhongshan are each assigned 200,000, Dongguan, Shunde, and Xinhui are each assigned 150,000, Chao'an, Jieyang, Chaoyang, and Chenghai are each assigned 120,000. The largest quota is for Taishan, which is assigned 250,000. The remaining counties, with quotas of tens of thousands or thousands, are assigned specific quotas for selling bonds and remitting funds. (August 16)

Fujian Army Begins Troop Movements 77

剿匪 Campaign About to Launch

Fuzhou Correspondent: The various army units of Fujian Province and the 19th Route Army are now carrying out troop movements in sequence. The city of Fuzhou and its surrounding suburbs are to be guarded by the Supplementary Brigade of the 19th Route Army, under Tan Qixiu. The 1st Marine Brigade, under Liu Gangde, which was originally stationed in the Qiaonan district of the city, has moved to the southern countryside. The Engineer Battalion of the 56th Division, which was stationed in the Qiaobei district, has moved to the western countryside. The 2nd Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army, under Chen Qixuan, which was stationed in the urban area, has moved to the northern countryside. The troop movements have been underway for several days. As for the defense of southern Fujian, the 1st Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army, under Chen Guohui, also began to withdraw from Huian, Nan'an, and Anxi on the previous day, in accordance with orders, to be replaced by the Mao Weishou Division of the 19th Route Army, and moved into Yongchun, Dehua, and Datian. However, the people of these three counties, in view of the illegal activities of the Chen Brigade in the Quanzhou area, strongly opposed it, and sent telegrams to the Pacification Commissioner's Office, the Provincial Government, and the Headquarters of the 19th Route Army, refusing the entry of the Chen Brigade. At the same time, the people of the Xianyou and Tian counties, because the deputy brigade commander of the 3rd Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army, He Xianzhu, forced the planting of opium seedlings and extorted military pay, amounting to 5 million yuan in just three years, which the people could not bear, also suddenly launched an anti-He movement. Representatives were elected by various groups to come to the province to organize a Save-Our-Homeland Association, demanding that the Pacification Commissioner's Office investigate He and send the 19th Route Army to take over the defense. The storm is quite intense.

After the 60th Division of the 19th Route Army, under Shen Guanghan, and the 78th Division, under Qu Qingnian, were stationed in Longyan and Yongding counties, the overall offensive was temporarily postponed because the armies of Jiangxi and Guangdong provinces had not yet arrived at the agreed locations. First, scattered bandits in the rear were searched for, and economic blockade was strictly enforced, causing panic in the bandit areas. Now, Commander-in-Chief Cai Tingkai, having received a telegram from Military Affairs Committee Chairman Jiang, instructed the Shen and Qu divisions to actively advance towards their destinations and change their previous guerrilla tactics. After receiving the order, Cai ordered the Shen Division to advance towards Changting from Shizhong, and the Qu Division to advance towards Changting from Kanshi, in preparation for the overall offensive. At the same time, he telegraphed the Guangdong forces stationed in Shanghang and Wuping counties, requesting them to postpone their withdrawal so that the army could concentrate its forces for battle. Yesterday, he received a reply telegram from Chen Jitang, approving the retention of Yan Yingyu's brigade in Wuping and Zhong Shaokui's unit in Shanghang to assist in defense. Also, the 19th Route Army's military pay, which was originally allocated 300,000 yuan per month by the Central Government and 200,000 yuan per month by Guangdong, has been specially approved by the Central Government to increase by 200,000 yuan per month, starting in August, and by Guangdong to increase by 100,000 yuan, for application, but all for a limited period of three months. (August 19)

A Glimpse of the Stele Forest On the afternoon of the 14th, we made a brief visit to the Stele Forest, a historically famous site in Xi'an. Upon entering, we saw steles everywhere, a dazzling array that made us reluctant to leave. Among the many steles, the Sacred Teaching Preface Stele, the Nestorian Stele, the Yan Family Temple Stele, and the Thirteen Classics Stele were particularly well-known. According to our guide, there are about 2,000 steles, divided into more than 440 types. A full set of the Thirteen Classics Stele sells for 85 yuan. The stones, totaling two hundred forty-five, with over one hundred seventy补 stones, are each about six尺 tall and two尺 six寸 wide, contains about three thousand six hundred and fifty-six characters, and sells for about thirty-five yuan. We contemplated them for a long time, but ultimately decided that this matter was outside the scope of our investigation and we could not devote enough time to its study. We then visited the Confucius Temple, inspected the ancient sacrificial vessels such as 籩豆 housed there, and returned.

Approaching Our Destination That evening, Provincial Government members and directors Zhao Shouyu, Li Bailing, Han Guangqi, Li Zhigang, Li Xie, Yu Jun, and others hosted a banquet for all of us at the Northwest Hotel. This was our only banquet together. Tomorrow morning, the members of our North and South groups would head to their respective destinations. The North Group's scope of investigation included sixteen counties: Sanyuan, Yao County, Tongguan, Yijun, Zhongbu, Luochuan, Kuang County, Ganquan, Fushi, Yanchang, Yichuan, Jiyi Town, Longmen, Hancheng, Lin Yang, and Dali. The South Group's scope of investigation included nineteen counties: Qinling, Xiaoyi, Zhen'an, Ankang, Hanyin, Shiquan, Xixiang, Chenggu, Hanzhong, Mian County, Baozhong, Liuba, Miaotaizi, Feng County, Jianchawei, Baoji, Fengxiang, Wugong, and Xingping. The route seemed longer for the South Group, but the scenery along the way was better, and there were many more famous scenic spots and historical sites. The North Group's investigation period was five days shorter than the South Group's, but the journey would be more arduous.

For the convenience of work, each group was further divided into eight subgroups: agriculture and forestry, mining, industry and commerce, water conservancy, transportation, economy, special products, and education. On the North Group side, Li Yongzhen, Sun Zhongyi, and Gu Zhizhong joined the agriculture and forestry group; Huang Bokui, Hu Boyuan, Ma Jin, and Feng Jinglan joined the mining group; Yu Qianliu, Xu Nanchou, and Zhu Ruijie joined the water conservancy group; Liu Binglun and Hua Chenghou joined the transportation group; Xu Yihe and Bian Wenjian joined the economy group; Yan Wei joined the special products group; and Gu Zhizhong and Zhang Mofu joined the education group. The South Group's arrangements were not yet finalized as of this writing. According to the director's announcement, we would get up at 7:00 AM on the 15th, have breakfast at 8:00 AM, and set off at 9:00 AM, and depart at 10:00 AM.

On the 15th, we got up at 6:00 AM, and by 7:00 AM, the sound of people was everywhere. Three hours later, the North Group would set off for Sanyuan, and the South Group would set off for Qinling. According to Zhao Shouyu, the places we had passed through before were mostly paradise, but from here on, we would be heading towards hell. But what the taste of hell is like, listen to the next installment.

Also, since the reporter has joined the North Group, aside from entrusting someone to write reports on the South Group, all correspondence will be limited to the North Group. As for the omissions regarding the various situations in Xi'an, I plan to supplement them upon my return. (Sent from Xi'an at 8:00 AM on August 15)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 79

Cao Regiment Transferred to Siyang to Suppress Bandits Cao Pang, the commander of the 2nd Security Regiment of Jiangsu Province, has been stationed in Songjiang for two years. He has rectified his troops and eliminated the gangs in Pudong, and is well-loved by the local people. During the Japanese invasion of Shanghai this year, Commander Cao spared no effort in maintaining local order, sending troops to build roads. The people were able to live in peace. It is learned that the province has ordered him to transfer to Siyang to suppress bandits. Various organizations and district chiefs in the county have sent telegrams to the Provincial Security Department, pleading for him to stay, but have not been successful. In addition to ordering his troops to prepare for departure, Commander Cao will retain several companies in Songjiang to console the people. He has also scheduled a farewell gathering at the auditorium of the People's Education Center on the 23rd, inviting people from all walks of life to attend and bid farewell. Various local organizations have been hosting banquets for several days to express their farewell sentiments.

Suzhou 80

Police Squad Vigorously Suppresses Lake Bandits On the 27th of the previous month, a large group of Pudong gang bandits suddenly arrived at Chenmu Longting Town in Suzhou, kidnapping seven villagers: Shen Changbao, Shen A'san, Shen A'xi, Zhang Erbao, Jiang Zhangshi, Jiang Gushi, and Xu Xiangxing. The families of the hostages later received letters from the bandits, requesting ransom payments on the 20th (the previous day) by the Xiao Dian Lake. This was detected by the Second Squadron of the County Police, stationed in the village, and Ma, the squadron leader, immediately dispatched Team Leader Wang to lead a team to suppress the bandits and rescue the hostages. Upon arriving at the destination, they were informed by the villagers that there were indeed four bandit boats lingering there. Team Leader Wang then ordered one policeman to be left on each boat to guard it, and the rest of the team landed and advanced. They saw a large crowd of villagers gathered and inquired whether there were any bandits, but all claimed ignorance, so they continued to advance. Unexpectedly, the bandits were mixed in with the crowd, intimidating the villagers from reporting. Seeing that the police had passed, the bandits gathered and opened fire on the boats the police had arrived on. Zhang Jinquan, who was guarding a boat at the time, was wounded in the leg. Upon hearing the gunshots, Team Leader Wang quickly ordered a counterattack. The bandits also opened fire to resist. The two sides exchanged fire for two hours, but the bandits did not retreat. Fortunately, Squadron Leader Ma led his team to reinforce them, and the bandits were defeated and retreated towards Cheng Lake. In the battle, a bandit named Zhang Binwu, who confessed to being a low-level leader in the gang, was wounded and died soon after from his injuries. Squadron Leader Ma immediately sent the wounded policeman to Boji Hospital for treatment and reported the bandit suppression to the headquarters. However, a large number of hostages have not yet been rescued.

Capture of Fu Yongyan, Robber from Shengkang Village, Shaoxing 81

Xu Bingren, an investigator sent by the Shaoxing County Government, captured Fu Yongyan (also known as Ying Ting), a robber involved in the robbery case of Shengkang Village in Shaoxing County, in Room 15 of the Mingli Inn outside of Changmen. 245 yuan in banknotes, two pawn tickets, two customs treasury notes, and other items were found in his suitcase. He was immediately handed over to the police and taken to the Third Branch. The suspect confessed to the robbery without denial. The suspect was then handed over to the investigator to be taken back for investigation.

New Developments in the Murder of the Opium Partner Case Zheng Wanglong, the main seller, beat to death his opium partner, Wang Xinyuan (also known as Wang Xinyuan, or Xiao Wang). The Public Security Bureau has sent Zheng Wang to the court for trial and detention. The deceased's wife has arrived from Shanghai and hired lawyer Xu Junyan to submit a petition to the District Procuratorate, seeking justice for her husband. Because the autopsy at the time showed that the death was due to an epidemic, the coffin may be opened for another examination to clarify the truth.

Changzhou 82

County Middle School Student Kidnapped and Escapes Zhang Zuxun, a student at Wu Yi County Middle School, is the 18-year-old son of Zhang Renfu, the former assistant of the Fourth District Office. He lives in Tianhuangtang Alley in the city. On the 15th of this month, Zuxun went to the East Gate for sightseeing and was kidnapped by bandits. His family was very anxious because he had not returned for several days. However, he felt quite tired after walking from the countryside to the city.

Yang Haoming, the Director of the Education Bureau, feels that it is really difficult to maintain the situation and had previously submitted his resignation, which was not approved. Recently, Director Yang submitted another resignation to the county government for submission to the Education Department, stating that until a replacement is appointed, Supervisor Sun Youguang will act as his agent.

Wuxi 83

Central Committee Member Cai Yuanpei Comes to Wuxi to Escape the Noise There has been talk recently that Cai Yuanpei, a member of the Central Committee and President of the Academia Sinica and Chairman of the Central University Reorganization Committee, will succeed Wang Jingwei as President of the Executive Yuan. Although various parties have high hopes for him, Cai remains detached and has not agreed. The other day, he quietly left Shanghai and came to Wuxi by car, staying at the home of a friend with the surname of a certain someone in the city. He traveled lightly and kept his whereabouts secret. When someone visited him, he said that the actual political responsibility of the Executive Yuan was too much for him, as he was old and weak and difficult to shoulder this burden. Therefore, he has come to this place of scenic beauty to rest and recuperate. He will return to Nanjing soon, as Central University urgently needs reorganization. However, the exact date of his return to Nanjing is still difficult to determine for the time being. As for the recently discovered Blood Soul Extermination Groups and other things, they are also a manifestation of the patriotism of the Chinese people. However, it is necessary to persist, act according to the law, unite with sincerity, and be unyielding. Only then can we achieve the final victory, and even strong armor and sharp weapons are not to be feared.

Danyang 85

Kidnapping Case Occurs in Huashi Township The family of Deng Tingliang in Laoyashan Village, Huashi Township, Tenth District, was enjoying the cool air outside their door at about 10 p.m. last night (the 20th) when several bandits suddenly arrived, each holding guns and sharp weapons, and forbade them from making any noise. They kidnapped Deng's seven-year-old boy and carried him away. Deng, in desperation, chased after them. The bandits fired a shot backward, and the bullet grazed Deng's face, causing minor injuries. In the end, the boy was still taken away. The case has been reported to the police for investigation.

Gaoyou 86

Yun Gong Bureau Orders Demolition of Houses Along the Dike The Jiangbei Canal Engineering Bureau issued an order to the County Government yesterday, stating that it had investigated the construction of houses by the people in the Gaobao area, occupying the canal dikes and hindering the dike reconstruction work. The Yun Gong Association has already issued orders to the Gao and Bao counties, in accordance with the regulations set by the department for prohibiting the construction of houses on the top of the dike, to send police to order the demolition. It was found yesterday that the houses of the people along the dikes in Sishui in Bao County and Gaoyou have not been completely demolished, which is detrimental to flood prevention work. The County Government is hereby ordered to immediately dispatch police to demolish all houses along the dikes in its jurisdiction, whether newly built or old, and to ensure that nothing remains, in order to strengthen the dikes.

Funing 87

Eastern Township Discovery of Young Locusts: In the sixth district of this county, areas such as Huayuantou and Zhuhuitang have recently seen outbreaks of young locusts. The affected area is estimated to be several thousand acres. The locusts' heads have already turned red, and they are about to take flight. Farmers who witness this situation are filled with worry. Upon learning of this, the County Agricultural Experiment Station immediately dispatched assistant staff members Yao Yuqiu and Teng Fengji yesterday (the 16th) to rush to the area and guide the farmers in devising methods to eradicate the locusts.

To the Editor: We were astonished to read in your August 19th issue's Taicang local correspondence, under the headline "Patriotic Organizations Established One After Another," a report stating that the Youth Suicide Corps issued a severe warning to Wanhexiang Southern Goods Store for privately importing Japanese goods, and that upon investigation, two bullets were attached to the warning. Since the September 18th Incident, our store has indeed stopped buying and selling enemy goods, which can be verified. Moreover, at this time of national crisis, all people with a sense of righteousness are filled with grief and indignation and share the same hatred for the enemy. Our store's patriotism will certainly not lag behind others. Our conscience is clear and can be attested by Heaven and the sun. Furthermore, our store only received a warning letter from the Blood Soul Kill Traitors Corps, telling us to seal up the enemy goods we had previously stored. We did not receive any warning from the Youth Suicide Corps or the two bullets. This must be a misunderstanding. As it concerns our store's reputation, we respectfully request a correction. Wanhexiang Southern Goods Store, Shatou, Taicang, respectfully submitted on August 20th.

Shen Siliang Reports on China's Situation at the World Sports Conference in Los Angeles 90

China Is an Infant in the World of Sports

But Educators Are Aware of the Importance of Physical Education

Mexico Uses Sports to Eliminate a Century of Warfare

(Special Dispatch from Los Angeles) The World Sports Conference, sponsored by the American National Athletic Association, was held in Los Angeles starting on July 25th, taking advantage of the World Olympics in Los Angeles. It brought together sports experts from around the world. Shen Siliang represented China at the conference and reported on the current state of sports in China on the first day of the conference, describing the situation as follows:

A Total of 29 Countries Participated 91

A total of 29 countries participated in the conference, which lasted for five days from July 25th. The topics discussed were all related to the improvement of sports worldwide, such as "Civilian Sports," "Rural Sports," "Worker Sports," "Family Sports," and "Arts and Crafts and Sports," etc.

The Advocacy of Civilian Sports 92

On the morning of the first day, small group discussions were held first. Dr. CDeim, Director of the German National Sports Committee, advocated that civilian sports should have a central sports field in every location, so that parents and children can exercise together in one place.

Mexican Sports Eliminate War 93

LA Gayon, Director of Public Sports in Mexico, reported on the state of sports in Mexico. The promotion of sports in Mexico has eliminated the wars that politicians have failed to resolve for a century and has progressed rapidly. Young people across the country have gained mutual understanding through sports competitions and have connected with the world.

Italian Natural Movement 94

After the small group discussions, a general meeting was held. G. T. Kirby, treasurer of the American National Athletic Association, presided over the meeting. J. S. Edstrom, a member of the Swedish Olympic Committee, reported on the state of sports in Sweden. Mr. Edstrom is the manager of a Swedish electrical company. Colonel M. Serrati, the Italian representative, reported on sports in Italy, saying that the natural movement of sports throughout Italy has created an absolutely correct personality uplift.

Shen Siliang Reports on China's Situation 95

Shen Siliang, the Chinese representative, then reported on the state of sports in China, saying that China is only an infant in the world of sports, but educators across the country are aware of the supreme importance of physical education and are discussing ways to promote and improve it.

Worker Sports and Family Sports 96

Small group discussions were held again in the afternoon, with the themes of worker sports and family sports. Regarding worker sports, L. Mabnuson, director of the International Labor Bureau in Washington, and Miss A. Henry, representative of the Australian Sports Ground Committee, said that due to the surplus free time gained in the machine age, workers today are studying how to make it a happier and more proper use. Regarding family sports, Dr. K. R. VonHaet, a German lawyer, banker, and Olympic team leader, said that it is most urgent to restore the physical strength and interest lost by a family due to a day's work. Ms. Taifo, representative of the British Parents Education Association, said that family sports are a preparation for children to enter the race of life in the future.

Discussion on Children's Sports 97

C. Bariolme, acting director of physical education at the University of the Philippines, discussed in detail how schools can allow children to use space and time. Dr. J. L. Merian's discussion focused on the value of children's sports for spatial life.

At the evening lecture, Dr. R. B. VonKleinSmid of Germany spoke on the topic of "The Possibility of Sports Promoting International Goodwill." The lecture was followed by dancing, and the meeting adjourned. The 26th was the second day, and there will be four small group discussions. In the afternoon, there will be a tour of Hollywood and the famous beaches of Beverly Hills.

National Physical Education Implementation Plan (Continued from Yesterday) 98

(II) Facilities

School Physical Education Facilities

(A) Fields: divided into ball games, track and field, equipment, national martial arts, and playgrounds. The size and quantity should be sufficient to implement the physical education curriculum standards for all levels of schools, with a standard of at least 100 square feet of open space for each student.

(B) Buildings: All buildings necessary for implementing the curriculum, such as gymnasiums, covered playgrounds, swimming pools, physical examination rooms, and medical rooms, should be built according to their capabilities.

(C) Equipment: All fixed and consumable equipment required for the curriculum and extracurricular activities should be fully equipped.

Sports Field Facilities

The area of the county sports field should be at least 30 mu, and the area of the provincial or executive Yuan-administered municipal sports field should be at least 80 mu. The construction and setting of various sports fields should be fully constructed according to the interests and needs of the entire county's population.

Simple sports fields can be more simply constructed according to the needs of the surrounding people.

Children's playgrounds should be fully equipped with children's play equipment and use them as a principle.

(III) Funding

The original proposal is revised as follows:

(1) The physical education funding for schools at all levels, in addition to the physical education fees paid by students, must account for at least 3% of the school's recurring expenses, but the salaries of physical education teachers and staff and special construction are not included.

(2) The recurring expenses of sports fields in each province, city, and county should account for at least 10% of the social education expenses of each province, city, and county, but construction and fixed equipment expenses are not included.

IV. Part on Implementation Methods (1) Research Work 99

The materials used for physical education, the methods adopted, and the standards set must go through research procedures before they can comply with scientific principles and be timely. Therefore, research is the first step in promoting physical education. If it is abandoned, it is like a blind man riding a blind horse, and it is feared that it will mislead people.

A. The research institutions may have the following types:

(1) Establish a Central Physical Education Research Institute.

(2) The Cultural Foundation sets up physical education lectures to assist the physical education department of a university in conducting research work.

(3) Designate domestic educational research and experimental institutions to add physical education research departments, and the Ministry of Education will subsidize the expenses.

(4) Select model towns and villages as physical education experimental areas.

(5) National Martial Arts Museum.

B. Research Matters

(1) The physical education curriculum standards for all schools with a systematic approach shall be researched and compiled by the Physical Education Curriculum Standards Committee established by the Ministry of Education, designated for implementation and experimentation in various schools, and then promulgated and adopted after satisfactory results are obtained. (2) Various standards.

1. The items and standards for physical education assessment, including skills, physical fitness, testing, and other standards obtained from testing statistics.

2. Standards of physical fitness

(3) National martial arts. The similarities and differences between the principles and schools of national martial arts, the methods of teaching and competition, and the status and value of physical education must be jointly studied and planned by national martial artists and physical educators.

(4) Rural education. 85% of our people live in rural areas and are mostly engaged in agriculture. Do they have spare time to engage in physical education? What kind of activities do they like? On-site investigation and research should be conducted.

(5) Industrial and commercial physical education. Search for appropriate methods to enable workers and merchants to receive physical education training.

(6) Game materials. Collect old physical activities of the people, improve and promote them, and adopt foreign mass physical activities to adapt to the Chinese environment and use them flexibly.

(7) Scope of women's sports.

(8) Other

(II) Teacher Training 100

A. Training Institutions

(1) University and high school teachers, physical education administrators, and physical education field instructors.

1. National Institute of Physical Education (using the Central Physical Education Field)

2. Each university should establish a physical education department.

(2) Junior high school and elementary school teachers, county physical education service personnel, and junior physical education administrators.

1. High school normal schools or normal schools should set up physical education courses. In the first academic year, they will be the same as ordinary courses. From the second academic year, they will specialize in physical education academic courses. The itinerary will be determined separately.

2. Provincial Physical Education College.

B. Training Course

There are many subjects in the physical education curriculum itself and its related subjects. The necessary ones are listed below, and the percentage of the total curriculum is indicated for reference. The physical education curriculum of normal schools can be selected for the necessary subjects.

(1) Biological subjects, including anatomy, physiology, hygiene, first aid, massage, health inspection, and sports physiology, account for 19%.

(2) Educational sciences, including the outline of education, educational psychology, educational law, educational administration, educational philosophy, health education, and police investigation principles, account for 15%.

(3) Physical education theory, including physical education principles, game principles, physical education administration, physical education teaching methods, elementary school textbooks, kinesiology, physical education history, and mass physical education, account for 20%.

(4) Technical subjects account for 21%.

(5) Cultural subjects and electives account for 25%.

C. Further Study Methods

(1) Use summer school, summer training courses, and summer tutoring classes.

(2) Send people abroad for observation and study.

1. Select physical education personnel who have served for many years and have excellent achievements to go to various countries for on-site observation and research on a regular basis.

(2) When each province sends students to study abroad, it should carefully select excellent physical education personnel with both academic and sports skills to be sent to study abroad.

3. The Ministry of Education and various provinces should list physical education quotas when holding study abroad examinations.

V. Implementation Methods 101

A. School Physical Education

(1) University education colleges, high school normal schools, and rural teachers and model schools should add physical education as a required subject to cultivate the ability to assist extracurricular activities.

(2) Physical education curriculum (including national martial arts)

(1) Before the promulgation of the university physical education curriculum standards, each school should formulate its own detailed items for trial implementation, two hours per week. Those who fail the exam shall not be promoted or graduate.

(2) Primary and secondary normal schools shall be handled in accordance with the temporary curriculum standards of the Ministry of Education. Those who fail the exam shall not be promoted or graduate.

(3) Physical Education Materials (including national martial arts)

The Ministry of Education shall set up a physical education textbook editing committee to compile it.

(4) Teacher qualifications

(1) University and high school physical education teachers shall be filled by those who have obtained degrees from universities at home and abroad.

(2) Junior high school and elementary school physical education teachers shall be filled by graduates of provincial physical education colleges, high school normal schools, or normal school physical education departments. (5) Teacher treatment,

(1) Reward physical education inventors and stipulate pension and bereavement regulations, and issue them to the whole country.

(2) The salary standards for morning exercises and extracurricular activities in schools at all levels shall be calculated in the same way as regular classes.

B. Mass Physical Education 102

(1) The method of carrying out the business of provincial, municipal, and county sports fields

(1) Daily guidance work should be scheduled so that it is easy to train and easy to manage. (See the attached table for reference)

(2) Children should be gathered at a scheduled time to carry out group activities such as徒手游, equipment games, singing, dancing, and storytelling. (3) Women should be gathered at a scheduled time to carry out regular track and field games, ball games, equipment, and gymnastics training.

(4) Adults should be gathered and guided at a scheduled time according to the types of activities in this field, or they should be temporarily organized to compete with each other, or the skills of fitness should be instructed separately, so that they can practice automatically.

(5) After the daily guidance work is completed, the teaching methods and materials used on that day should be recorded as required for research and to determine the most effective method of their work.

(6) For competitive sports such as track and field games, ball games, etc., public competitions should be held at least once a year according to different seasons. It is especially good to hold those who can hold degrees and qualifications separately. Other physical education-related events, such as children's health competitions and posture competitions, should also be held more often to promote them with facts.

(7) The public, especially farmers and businessmen, should seize every opportunity to use various propaganda methods to arouse their interest and attention in order to stimulate their preference for physical education.

(8) Various groups such as outing groups, hunting groups, picnic groups, and walking groups should be organized at any time to increase the interest in social leisure life.

(9) Collect the opinions of the public on sports events, investigate the personal history of those who come to the field for sports, and the progress of social physical education for reference in research and improvement.

(10) Network and assist local and other sports organizations or schools to expand the effectiveness of activities. (The above are the common points of the provincial, municipal, and county sports fields).

(11) Research and experiment on new physical education projects that meet the needs of society (12) Guide and assist the county sports field in carrying out its work (the special work of the provincial public sports field)

This standard shall be implemented with the approval of the Ministry of Education.

(2) To promote mass physical education in the physical education experimental area, 1. Each province and city must establish one physical education experimental area from the 21st year, and the period is temporarily set at two years (the county in which it will be held will be designated by the Department of Education).

2. From the 23rd year, the methods implemented in the experimental area will be popularized to the provinces, cities, and counties, and at the same time, they will be popularized to the whole country.

3. The administrative personnel in the experimental period of two years are as follows:

(1) The Department of Education specially hires one expert.

(2) One physical education instructor from the County Education Bureau.

(3) One cadre specially assigned by the Mass Education Center and the Farmers Education Center.

(4) A number of public security bureau health police.

(5) Appoint two to three cadres.

(6) One specially appointed district teacher.

4. The salaries of the staff are only provided by the experimental area for the assigned cadres and specially appointed doctors, and the salaries of the remaining staff are paid by the original agency.

5. The annual expenses are managed by the Department of Education during the experimental period. After two years of popularization, they will be paid by the Education Bureau and included in the budget.

6. The administrative system of the experimental area is as follows:

Department of Social Education of the Ministry of Education, Section Chief of the Third Section of the Department of Education, various shares of physical education, health cadres, propaganda and assistant general affairs personnel, etc.

7. The site of the experimental area is located in the sports field.

8. The business of the experimental area is as follows:

(1) Hold mass amateur sports meetings two to four times a year.

(2) Hold various ball games competitions.

(3) Organize national martial arts classes (such as Chinese New Martial Arts Tai Chi exercises, all those that meet scientific principles can be adopted.

(4) Organize various fitness groups (such as business people who have free time in the morning, organize business people's morning exercise classes, etc.)

(5) Circulating physical education and national martial arts guidance.

(6) Hold the following health competitions separately each year:

1. Adult male health competition.

2. Adult women's health competition.

3. Children's health competition.

(7) Physical education lectures.

(8) Physical education wall newspapers.

(9) Physical education exhibitions.

(10) Physical education publishing house.

3. The field director and instructors of the sports field in each province, city, and county must be graduates of the physical education department of the university, the physical education college, or the physical education department of the high school normal school with a considerable degree.

4. Various gatherings

(1) The National Games are held every two years and are held in rotation in various provinces and cities designated by the National Sports Committee.

(2) The Provincial and Municipal Games are held once a year, and the methods are determined by the Sports Committee of the Provincial and Municipal Education Bureaus.

(3) Sports meetings are held once a year at all levels of schools.

(Nearby) 1. A national martial arts item should be added to various sports meetings. 2. The athletes participating in sports meetings at all levels must first undergo academic, moral, age, physical fitness, and amateur review. The standards and methods shall be studied and stipulated by the National Sports Committee.

(IV) Regulations 103

(1) The organization of various sports federations, whether temporary or fixed, must be filed with the competent education authority according to the following standards: 1. The purpose is pure and purely amateur in nature.

2. The competition must have appropriate age and gender classifications.

3. The responsible organizers must have served in the physical education field for more than two years and have considerable achievements.

4. The participating units are indeed representative of educational or vocational institutions and are not engaged in sports as a profession and do not hinder the amateur spirit.

5. There is a definite funding source and the income from tickets is not used as maintenance fees.

(2) If the above-mentioned registered groups continue to operate for three years and the competent education authority reviews and believes that they have considerable achievements, they may be given spiritual and material assistance. If there is any violation of the above-mentioned regulations after registration, they may be punished. The punishment methods shall be handled separately according to the severity of the circumstances.

(3) Various technical observation groups must have the following qualifications to be registered with the competent education authority:

(1) Members all have legitimate occupations and are not engaged in sports as a profession.

(2) There are physical education experts serving as instructors.

(3) Participation in various competitions or sports does not use ticket income as maintenance or apportioned to members.

(4) Members only have the obligation to pay fees when joining the association and do not enjoy material rights.

4. If the above-mentioned groups have special achievements after registration, they may be given considerable rewards. If there is any violation of the above-mentioned regulations, their group and the amateur qualifications of all its members will be revoked.

(5) Groups in items (1) and (13) that have not been registered with the competent education authority shall not participate in various gatherings and competitions organized by educational institutions and registered groups.

(6) Any organization that aims to study physical education academics and has made definite achievements may be registered with the education authority in accordance with the methods for academic groups and may be given considerable subsidies.

(7) In areas where there are no physical education organizations, the competent education authority shall convene people in the physical education field to promote the organization.

(8) Any registered group may report to the competent education authority in advance for review and consider subsidies when participating in international gatherings or sports meetings.

(9) Various groups shall not participate in political activities in the name of the group. 5. Assessment Methods The assessment of physical education and sports meetings have opposite positions. Sports meetings assess personal achievements, which are only enough to promote the progress of personal achievements. It is a mistake to use this as a standard for evaluating the entire physical education of schools and the public, and to use it as a tool for promotion, in order to promote the popularization of physical education in schools and the public is like seeking fish from trees. On the other hand, physical education assessment is to examine the physical education achievements of the entire city of schools or cities, which can urge the progress of physical education for the majority of the people, and to use this as a means to evaluate the physical education of schools or cities is very reliable.

Section A: Committee for Performance Evaluation 104

(1) The national physical education performance evaluation is to be presided over by the National Physical Education Committee. (1) Evaluate the physical education of all national universities and registered private universities in the country, determine their order of merit, and announce the results. (2) Determine the physical education performance of each province and announce the results.

(2) The physical education performance evaluation of each city and province is to be presided over by the Provincial Physical Education Committee.

(1) Examine the physical education performance reports of all provincial secondary schools, normal schools, and vocational schools and report to the Department of Education.

(2) Examine the physical education performance of graduates of provincial senior and junior secondary schools, normal schools, and vocational schools.

(3) Examine the public physical education in various provincial cities and report the proportion and number of examinees who passed the exam and participants to the Department of Education.

(3) The physical education performance evaluation of each county and city is to be presided over by the Education Bureau of each county and city or the Physical Education Committee of neighboring counties.

1. Examine the physical education performance of county-run primary and secondary schools within the county, determine their order of merit, and announce the results, and report the performance of secondary schools to the Department of Education.

(2) Examine the physical education performance of graduating students from senior and junior secondary schools, normal schools, and vocational schools within the county.

(3) Examine the performance of public physical education within the county and report to the Department of Education. Item B: The evaluation items are to be stipulated by the Central Physical Education Research Institute. Item C: The evaluation standards are to be researched and stipulated by the Central Physical Education Research Institute. Item D: The types of evaluation.

(1) Graduation Examinations for Students of All Levels

1. In primary schools, students who fail to meet the primary school physical education standards shall not be allowed to graduate.

2. In secondary schools, normal schools, and vocational schools, students who fail to meet the secondary school physical education standards shall not be allowed to graduate.

3. In universities, students who fail to meet the university physical education standards shall not be allowed to graduate.

(2) School Physical Education Performance Examinations

1. Primary schools: to be implemented by the Physical Education Committee of each county and city, with the Education Bureau evaluating the order of merit and announcing the results.

2. Secondary schools, normal schools, and vocational schools: to be implemented by the Provincial or County/City Physical Education Committee, report to the Department of Education or Education Bureau, and the Department of Education or Education Bureau will determine and announce the results.

3. Universities: the examination is to be implemented by the Physical Education Committee of the province where they are located, report to the Ministry of Education, and the Ministry of Education will determine and announce the results.

(3) Physical education must be a compulsory subject for all levels and types of examinations.

6. Phased Implementation Plan

The physical education facilities and promotion methods listed in this plan cannot be fully implemented immediately given the current situation in our country. Therefore, it is necessary to implement them in phases depending on the economic situation, available talent, and local conditions. A phased implementation plan is specially drafted for the reference of the competent authorities.

The following should be implemented in the first year:

1. Completion of central and local administrative organizations.

2. The regular physical education expenses of schools at all levels in cities must be implemented according to the established standards.

3. Establish physical education fields in major cities.

4. Establishment of a national research institute and commencement of research.

5. Promulgation of detailed curricula and standards for talent development. 6. Prepare for and operate summer schools.

7. Promulgation of measures for the registration and rewards of physical education organizations and implementation thereof.

8. Each province should appropriately set up items for physical education expenses.

9. Schools at all levels should appropriately increase physical education equipment.

10. Reinstate regulations stipulating that physical education is a compulsory subject in schools at all levels, and students who fail shall not be promoted or graduate.

12. Each province may conduct trial implementation of performance evaluation methods.

The following should be completed within the third year:

1. All kinds of research work should have considerable results reports and methods for promotion.

2. Establish physical education fields in each county.

3. Continue to supplement physical education equipment and experimental area work in schools at all levels. 4. The central government should send several physical education experts to various countries for research and investigation for a term of one year for the second time.

4. Conduct performance evaluations in major cities and towns.

The following should be completed within the fifth year:

1. Physical education fields in various villages.

2. Physical education equipment in schools at all levels should meet the standards of this plan. 3. Conduct national performance evaluations.

3. Research work should have considerable results.

The above plan should be supervised and implemented by the National Physical Education Committee. When the third year is completed, the second National Physical Education Conference should be convened to improve the subsequent implementation methods. (End)

Students' personalities will be identified, and the most appropriate guidance methods will be applied to ensure that each student has a sound personality.

Local News

Song Ziwen Flew to Shanghai Yesterday 129

To Carry Out the Collection of Paper Currency Tax

Banking Community Urges Postponement of Tax Collection, Possibly Approved

Currently Negotiating Loan with Various Banks

According to the Central News Agency, Minister of Finance Song Ziwen, after flying to Nanjing with Premier of the Executive Yuan Wang Jingwei to discuss the resignation of Wang and Zhang with Chairman Lin and Military Affairs Council Chairman Jiang, returned to Nanjing the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning at 8:20 AM, he, along with Director of the Department of Health Liu Ruiheng, Secretary Huang Chun Tao, Finance Department Advisor Qin Jingfu, and others, took a private Sikorsky airplane from Nanjing to Shanghai. Song's mission this time is to discuss the issue of collecting paper currency tax with the banking community in Shanghai. Details are as follows:

Consulting with Zhang Shouyong: After arriving in Shanghai yesterday morning, Song returned to his private residence on Qiqi Road for a short rest. At approximately 9:00 AM, he drove to visit Zhang Shouyong, Advisor to the Ministry of Finance, for about an hour to discuss the issue of collecting paper currency tax nationwide. Song, aware that the banking community in Shanghai is urging a postponement of the tax collection, but also realizing that the financial difficulties make the tax collection necessary, sought Zhang's opinion on this matter.

Banking Community's Opinion: A Central News Agency reporter interviewed a member of the Shanghai banking community yesterday to inquire about their opinion on the Ministry of Finance's collection of paper currency tax. According to them, various countries in Europe and America have certain regulations regarding the collection of paper currency tax from banks. For example, Bank A with a certain amount of capital is allowed to issue a certain amount of paper currency. If the amount of paper currency issued by that bank exceeds the prescribed amount, it will be taxed according to the promulgated paper currency tax regulations. Therefore, the banking community itself is not affected much. The paper currency tax promulgated by our country's Ministry of Finance on August 1, 1930, does not have such a provision. All banks that issue paper currency, regardless of the amount of paper currency issued, are taxed at 2.5% of the 40% reserve requirement of the paper currency issuance amount. If this regulation is followed, it will place a heavy burden on the banking community. In recent years, domestic wars and disasters have been frequent, and financial panic has reached its peak. The burden borne by the banking community is impossible to increase. Therefore, the Shanghai banking community is making every effort to urge a postponement of the Ministry of Finance's collection of paper currency tax. The estimated total amount of pure currency in the country is over 300 million yuan. Collecting according to the promulgated paper currency tax rate would yield over 3 million yuan annually. It is rumored that the total amount of paper currency in the country is 20 billion yuan, which is not true. A spokesperson for the Bankers Association told a Central News Agency reporter that they do not want to make any claims regarding the Ministry of Finance's planned implementation of the paper currency tax. The association has designated Zhang Gongquan of the Bank of China, Lu Jianquan of the Bank of Communications, and Hu Bijiang of the Zhongnan Bank to personally present a petition to Minister Song this afternoon to explain everything. However, as of the time of the interview (4:00 PM), they had not yet left. The contents of the petition are temporarily confidential. However, the banking community is truly unable to bear such a large tax burden due to the difficult times, and therefore requests that the tax collection be waived.

Significance of Paper Currency Tax: The spokesperson for the Bankers Association also said that paper currency tax is also implemented in various countries in Europe and America, but it is collected only on the amount of issuance that exceeds the prescribed issuance limit. The national banks strictly adhere to this regulation. For example, if the prescribed paper currency issuance limit for a certain bank is one million, if its paper currency increases to one million and several tens of thousands, then the excess of tens of thousands will be subject to a certain percentage of issuance tax. This is to control the excessive issuance of paper currency and also contains the meaning of business tax. Therefore, the burden on the banking industry is not considered too heavy.

Tax Rate: The spokesperson also said that the paper currency tax rate stipulated by the Ministry of Finance is 0.25% (2.5/1000), and its target of collection is the reserve portion of paper currency issuance, that is, 40% of the full amount. Therefore, calculated as a percentage of the full issuance amount, the percentage of collection is 1%. The current amount of paper currency in our country is over 300 million yuan. Calculated at 1%, the tax burden is approximately 3 million yuan per year. Under the current economic downturn, it is difficult for the banking industry to bear. Furthermore, there is no provision for the collection of paper currency tax from foreign banks. This kind of uneven tax collection will cause domestic banks to reduce their issuance to reduce their burden, while foreign banks will increase their issuance due to the profitability, and the result will be to destroy the meager achievements of the Chinese banking industry in the past ten years.

Difficulties with the General Treasury: A member of the banking community also said that today's newspaper reported a Nanjing dispatch that the Ministry of Finance, in order to maintain the credit of paper currency, decided to organize a general treasury for paper currency reserves, consisting of 60% of the cash reserves of various banks. The banking community believes this news to be a rumor. Each bank needs to have a cash reserve of over 60% when issuing paper currency in order to maintain its credit. Each bank is responsible for maintaining its own credit, and there is no reason to combine the reserves into one place. In fact, it is impossible to do so. Chen Weiqing's Remarks: Yesterday, the Central News Agency reporter visited Chen Weiqing, Secretary of the Ministry of Finance, at the Central Bank, and asked whether the Ministry of Finance's intention to establish a general treasury for cash reserves was accurate, and what the extent of the progress of the paper currency issuance tax collection was. According to Secretary Chen, he had not heard of the Ministry of Finance's intention to establish a general treasury for cash reserves and had only seen it in the newspapers. If the Ministry of Finance needs to establish a general treasury for cash reserves, it should consult with the banking community in advance, or solicit their opinions. But the Ministry of Finance and the banking community have not had any contact or solicitation regarding this matter so far. Therefore, the claim that it will be established on September 1, as reported in the newspaper, should be inaccurate. As for the Ministry of Finance's collection of paper currency issuance tax, the regulations were promulgated as early as August 1, 1930, but have not been implemented to this day. Recently, the Ministry of Finance, in order to prevent paper currency from flooding the market, decided to implement the paper currency issuance tax and has notified various banks accordingly. However, the banking community is currently requesting a postponement of the tax collection.

Finance Department Plans to Borrow Money: According to financial circles, the purpose of the Finance Department's current implementation of the paper currency issuance tax is to remedy the financial difficulties. The banking community's plea for a postponement of the tax collection may be approved by the Finance Department, but in order to resolve the financial difficulties, a remedy must be sought. This remedy has not yet been determined. The Finance Department intends to temporarily postpone the tax collection, but must first mortgage this tax revenue to the banking community. The tax revenue will be deducted and repaid after the tax collection begins at a later date. However, the banking community believes that the paper currency issuance tax has not yet been implemented, so it cannot be mortgaged. If the authorities are in financial difficulty, they can negotiate loans with various banks separately. Observing the current situation, the paper currency issuance tax may be temporarily postponed. In order to remedy the current financial difficulties, the Finance Department will negotiate loans with various banks separately.

The Red Blood Assassination Corps Throws a Bomb at the Asia Company 131

Bomb Explodes, Company's Glass Windows Shattered

Shop Assistant Liang Naihu Suffers Head Injury from the Blast

Japanese Marines Arrive at the Scene to Investigate

Taking Numerous Photographs of the Aftermath of the Explosion

Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the Asia Bookstore Company at the north end of the Sichuan Road Bridge in this city, due to selling "enemy goods" and ignoring warnings, was bombed by the Red Blood Assassination Corps. The blast injured shop assistant Ran Naihu and destroyed doors, windows, counters, etc. The detailed account of the incident is as follows:

Shop Owner Driven by Profit. The Asia Bookstore Company, located at No. 18-20 North Sichuan Road, was founded by Li Yaonan, a Cantonese. The interior was elaborately decorated, and the business was quite prosperous. However, the stationery and supplies inside were all products of the Japanese company 克利洋行(Keli 洋行), and it also sold Japanese 金箭牌(Jin Jianpai, Golden Arrow) and 拜羅(Bailuo) fountain pens. Li had profited handsomely from this. After the January 28th Incident and the signing of the ceasefire agreement, Li, believing the opportunity had returned, secretly imported a large batch of Japanese stationery, intending to profit by taking advantage of the autumn school opening season for various schools. However, the Red Blood Assassination Corps detected this. Around 8:00 PM on the 20th, they sent personnel with a warning letter to the company, instructing them to seal up all Japanese goods within 48 hours and issue a public apology, or face appropriate consequences. Li Yaonan ignored the letter. Therefore, the Red Blood Assassination Corps resorted to the final measure yesterday morning.

Sudden Bombing. Around 8:00 AM yesterday morning, the company's shop assistants, with no customers coming in, gathered in the shop to chat. Around 9:00 AM, a shop assistant named Liang Naihu returned to the shop from outside. A young man in a Western suit followed closely behind. Liang did not pay much attention at the time. However, as Liang entered the door, he saw the young man raise his hand inward, and a loud explosion occurred behind Liang. Instantly, iron fragments flew everywhere. The glass window counters on the left and in the middle facing the street, displaying Golden Arrow and Bailuo fountain pens, were shattered. A hole was blasted in the wooden board under the middle window counter. Liang's head was also injured by the iron fragments. The order in the shop was instantly disrupted, and the doors and windows were completely destroyed. The young man took the opportunity to escape at that moment.

Shop Assistant Injured. After the incident, nearby Chinese police officers on duty immediately reported to the Hongkou Police Station. They promptly dispatched personnel to the scene to investigate and collected the exploded iron fragments, taking them back to the police station for investigation. The injured shop assistant, Liang Naihu, was taken to the Fumin Hospital at Yokohama Bridge by the company itself. As the injuries were minor, the hospital doctor removed the iron fragments, applied medicine, and bandaged him. He returned to the company around 10:00 AM.

Japanese Side Pays Great Attention. After the police station inspected the scene, the Japanese Marines also arrived upon hearing the news. Two officers led guards directly to the company. At the same time, the Japanese Consulate also sent personnel to investigate the situation. They temporarily dispatched two Japanese soldiers to guard the entrance of the company, prohibiting people from coming and going nearby. Finally, the Japanese officers took many photographs of the bombed situation of the company, questioned the staff about the situation at that time, and so on.

At the foot of Mount Lushan in Jiangxi Province, there lived a farmer nicknamed Zhu Xiaogui. He married a local woman named Niu as his wife. Niu was somewhat attractive. Xiaogui had heard about it but was afraid of his wife's power and believed that family scandals should not be aired, so he did not interfere and let her do as she pleased. Xiaogui had an old mother who disapproved of the situation. However, she did not dare to directly scold them, only offering gentle advice. Niu, feeling ashamed and angered, saw her aunt as a thorn in her side. One night, she tricked her aunt into the room and strangled her to death with both hands. Xiaogui was gambling outside at the time and did not know the details. He believed Niu's story that his mother had died of a sudden illness.

Young Grandson Complains, Also Poisoned to Death. That night, she mixed arsenic into his food and forced him to swallow it. Thus, her son also died, bleeding from all seven orifices. The souls of the pitiful grandmother and grandson went to the King of Hell to seek justice.

Immortal Unhappy, Draws Sword to Help. At the time, Lü Dongbin had not yet attained enlightenment. He witnessed the events on Mount Lushan and wanted to seek justice, but he was instead attacked, his hands and feet bound, and thrown into a bottomless cave. Fortunately, He Xiangu rescued him and put the adulterous woman to death. The adulterer, due to some connection, escaped punishment.
