Free Talk

Two or Three Words

Locking up Nian Gengyao and Random Notes on the Western Campaign 177

— Zhanlu

The literary inquisitions of the early Qing Dynasty were very cruel, especially the case of Wang Jingqi, a recommended scholar from Qiantang, and his "Random Notes on the Western Campaign." Not only was Wang's family exterminated, but the Yongzheng Emperor was angered at other recommended scholars in Zhejiang. Therefore, in the fifth year of Yongzheng, an imperial edict was issued: "The scholars of Zhejiang have immoral habits, and the recommended scholars are suspended from the provincial examination." It was not until the eighth year of Yongzheng, Gengxu, that the recommended scholars of Zhejiang were allowed to participate in the provincial examination. This literary inquisition can be considered to have been handled on a very large scale.

Referring to the joint memorial of Fu Min, the Governor of Zhejiang, and E Mida, the General of Zhejiang, on October 17th of the third year of Yongzheng, we can see that the discovery of the "Random Notes on the Western Campaign" and the locking up of Nian Gengyao were related. The memorial stated:

"::: On September 28th, at Shenshi (3-5 PM), the Imperial Envoy and Minister of Leisure Duties, Dutong (Military Governor) Laxi, arrived in Hangzhou, bearing the imperial edict to lock up Nian Gengyao. Accordingly, that night, Dutong Laxi and I summoned Nian Gengyao to my office. I read the imperial edict aloud and immediately locked him up and placed him under guard. :::

::: Furthermore, we jointly searched Nian Gengyao's inner chambers and the letters in his study and kitchen cabinets, but found not a single piece of paper. We then interrogated his family members, who testified that Nian Gengyao had burned all his letters on September 12th. When we questioned Nian Gengyao, his confession was no different. After Laxi left, we conducted another detailed search of his heavy belongings and found two books of handwritten notes among the waste paper, titled "Reading Hall Random Notes on the Western Campaign." There was a preface by Wang Jingqi. Upon close examination, we found that what was said inside was rebellious. After secretly investigating the person for several days, we learned on October 16th that Wang Jingqi was Wang Riqi, a recommended scholar from Qiantang County. :::

At that time, Yongzheng was furious and wrote a rescript in red ink: "Two books of seditious words, temporarily retained." Although it was said to be "temporarily retained," this "Random Notes on the Western Campaign" was retained until after the Qing Dynasty was overthrown, when books from the imperial palace were scattered among the people, and the "Random Notes on the Western Campaign" became a book of tales. If Nian Gengyao had burned it at that time, Wang Jingqi's tragedy would have been avoided, and this "Random Notes on the Western Campaign" would have turned to ashes and could not have spread among the people.

Germany's Landscape Policy 178

— Shizi

The cleanliness of German streets has always been praised by the world.

Even the English, who pride themselves on being gentlemen, are ashamed of it. However, the cleanliness of German streets is not only true in cities but also in mountains and plains, especially in the management of scenery. Each state government has enacted special laws. All buildings of historical or scenic significance in the mountains and plains, whether publicly or privately owned, are not allowed to be damaged or demolished.

People who want to build a few houses by the mountains and rivers for their families to stay in during their free time, even if the land is privately owned, must first report to the Mountain Management Office. The experts of the office will carefully study it. If the plan does not harm the natural scenery, construction will be allowed. Otherwise, even if the house has been completed, it will be ordered to be demolished.

The reason for this is that Switzerland has beautiful mountains and rivers.

It was originally known as the park of Europe. However, since the Great War, all international conferences have been held there. Global dignitaries have come and gone, and those who like quiet have left. In addition, the cost of living has increased more than ever before. As a result, tourists have flocked north. The Germans, seeing an opportunity, have worked hard to attract tourists and promote the sale of goods and the prosperity of cities. Anything that can entertain tourists is vigorously pursued. Even advertising is strictly managed. Advertising signs are not allowed to be set up in places frequented by tourists, because they would obstruct the tourists' view and prevent them from fully appreciating the scenery of the lakes and mountains. A friend of mine once traveled to Germany and told me that he had traveled by train for one hour and twenty minutes and had seen only eleven advertising signs along the way. None of them were larger than ten square feet. Moreover, it is not known how much tax had to be paid for the permission of the managers to set up such advertising signs. The strictness of the management can be seen from this.

Recently, the Germans have been working harder to educate the children of the whole country about landscape policy. It is expected that in a few years, Germany's landscape policy will make even more amazing progress. Not only will it take over Switzerland's position, but I am afraid that all European tourists will be absorbed. Looking back at the countryside of our country, the roads are full of manure, which is disgusting. Even the Six Bridges and the Three Temples are full of villas on the lake and beggars on the mountains. How can we attract tourists? I know that the mountain spirits, if they knew, would also cry sadly.

Baishe Speaks 179

— Baishe

! Is it struggle or is it a charge?

! One of the great habits of the Chinese people!

Perhaps the Chinese cultivate a kind of ability to struggle in ordinary times? To put it more realistically, maybe they are practicing the skills of charging and fighting at any time and any place? Otherwise, why do they always try to be the first to get on the train, on the streetcar, and on the ship? You grab, and I grab, and in the end, it becomes a mess. In the end, no one can get on first?

I nagged my friends for more than half an hour about getting ahead, and what was the result? Just like a certain meeting, everyone patted their butts and left.

Now I will ask: "In the last earthquake in Japan, did more Chinese or Japanese die?" Maybe everyone will say in unison: "Of course more Japanese died, because the number of Chinese in Japan is far less than the number of local Japanese." However, according to the results of the most reliable investigations, there are opposite numbers. Where does this come from? The Japanese line up when they get on the ship, like ropes on a winch, smooth and unobstructed. What about the Chinese? They are huddled together like a stone cake. After a while, the stone cake turns into a pile of mountains. Is it possible to swallow the whole mountain in one bite? However, the more you can't swallow it, the bigger the area of the pile of mountains becomes. The organizational aspect also tends to be more and more tight in proportion, and finally becomes extremely solid. Naturally, it is impossible to swallow it in one bite, but the more you can't swallow it, the more I want you to swallow it. This shows the greatness of the Chinese people.

There are so many facts as right as this that they can be loaded in train cars,

But saying more may not help the real situation. What's more, now is a time of national crisis. This kind of struggle and charging training is also indispensable for the Chinese people, so I'm too lazy to drag it out.

Love of Birds 180

— Qian

"Their bodies lack the colored phoenix's nimble wings, but their hearts have the telepathic understanding."

From these two lines of poetry, we can see that the ancients had a considerable understanding of the love of birds. "The bridal tree still blends its branches, and the mandarin ducks do not sleep alone." This uses mandarin ducks as the representative of love.

In fact, love in birds is not limited to mandarin ducks. Love in birds is not just about flying together and sleeping together. Now I will give a few examples of facts that exist in slope situations.

(1) Kissing: Pigeons of both sexes kiss each other, which can often be seen. There is a kind of bird called the lovebird, the male and female never leave each other, and their beaks are always connected together.

(2) Singing: We buy a phonograph record in a shop and listen to him sing a few sentences of "I love you," "I love you," or "Love You Love You," a kind of crude singing. Compared with birds, it is really worlds apart. The beautiful sounds of birds, such as the lark, the oriole, and the thrush, are all admired by those who have heard them. Their songs are all for love.

(3) Modernization: Men and women strolling in the field of love all seek to be "modernized" in their clothes and costumes. This probably helps a lot in love. As for birds, since they don't have a penny to their name, where does modernization come from? The answer is: No. Birds are born modern. The peacock's brocade screen, the kingfisher's bright green, and the parrot's beautiful feathers are their heavenly

adornments.

(4) Dancing: A species of bird from Australia arranges a clean dance floor on the flat ground under the shade of trees. Or they specially build dance rooms decorated with branches, leaves, and bird feathers. However, birds only have two pairs of legs, unlike humans who also have two hands. Therefore, birds don't know any "Charleston" or waltzes." Their dancing is just opening their wings and fluttering back and forth, their feathers rubbing against each other.

A Spectator Who Slept for a Long Time 181

— Mianmian

Once, when the French theater in Paris was performing a work by the famous writer Orcia, the author of "La Dame aux Camélias," Alexander Dumas fils, who was sitting next to Orcia, saw a spectator sleeping in front of the stage. He pointed to this spectator and said to Orcia:

"Look! What is the effect of your work?"

Orcia was furious. Later, on the day when Dumas's work was being performed on the same stage, he was determined to find a sleeping spectator. Sure enough, he found a sleeping spectator in a seat close to the stage. He proudly pointed to this spectator and said to Dumas:

"Do you understand? This is the effect of your work." Dumas looked at this spectator and replied:

"Ah! I remember this person's face. He was the spectator that night. He hasn't woken up yet!"

A Secret History of the Twenty-One Demands (1) 182

— Si Ping

This secret history concerning the Twenty-One Demands that Japan presented to our nation in 1915 was dictated by the late Bishop Brent the year before his passing. However, it had never been published until recently. This article extensively clarifies the duplicity and fickleness of Japanese diplomacy and the world's concern for the Chinese issue. A verbatim translation of the original follows.

I have been overseeing Chinese missionary work since 1907. In the autumn of 1914, I traveled to Tokyo for church affairs. Bishop Harris asked if I would like to meet with then-Prime Minister of Japan, Marquis Ōkuma. I asked, "Was this meeting suggested by Marquis Ōkuma?" He laughed and said, "Yes." I replied that I would be very willing to speak with him and so a meeting was arranged for the following day.

The purpose of Marquis Ōkuma's meeting with me was to ask me to carry a message to China, urging China not to declare war or create disturbances due to the Japanese military's invasion of China. At that time, the Japanese army was preparing to attack Qingdao from the rear. This action by Japan was a violation of Chinese sovereignty, just as Germany violated Belgian sovereignty. During the meeting, Marquis Ōkuma said, "During my term as Prime Minister, I will never wage war against China." Later, he repeatedly declared, "As long as I am in office, Japan will never commit the great injustice of invading China."

After returning to China, I did not immediately convey Marquis Ōkuma's message to the Chinese government. During this time, I pondered how to offer China the best advice. At that moment, the Japanese Minister to China, Hioki Eki, came to see me, saying that he had just received a telegram from Marquis Ōkuma instructing him to visit me and ask me to restate the main points of Ōkuma's conversation with me.

I believed that Hioki Eki belonged to the pro-war faction, while Marquis Ōkuma belonged to the peace faction. Therefore, I clearly explained Ōkuma's promise to me. Hioki Eki asked me what kind of just attitude Japan should adopt towards China, Russia, and the United States. That afternoon, he spent half the day raising various questions on this topic and then listening to my opinions. I pointed out to him that Japan's proper policy should be to exert efforts to maintain peace with all countries, establishing itself as a leader in industry and commerce in the Far East and even the Pacific, just as Britain is a leader in industry and commerce in the Atlantic, and should not rely on military force to plot political hegemony.

I was eager to go to western China, so I packed my bags within three or four days. Before leaving, I went to the Japanese embassy to say goodbye to Hioki Eki and said to him that because I was in a hurry to leave now, I would return to visit him in the spring after returning from Sichuan.

After Hioki Eki visited, I went to see Tsai Ting-kan, telling him that I was there to convey a message from Japan, but that I could not be responsible for whether the message was truthful. I was merely like a postman. I then told him about my conversation with Marquis Ōkuma and my subsequent meeting with Hioki Eki. I thought Tsai Ting-kan must have conveyed this message to Yuan Shikai. Later, he came to talk to me a second time. Tsai Ting-kan told me that Yuan Shikai wanted to ask me whether Marquis Ōkuma could keep his word. I told him that I thought Marquis Ōkuma was sincere when he made this promise, and that he would be willing to abide by his promise as much as possible. However, in my opinion, he might be forced to make harsh demands on China, or he might have to resign,

allowing the military faction to take charge of the Japanese government.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

I Ask, What to Do? 183

— Buddha

Since the September 18th Incident, our side has strongly advocated recovering the lost territories of the Northeast, but to date, we have not seen a single soldier or general sent to recover the Northeast. However, the Japanese militarists' second and third steps of invasion are being revealed one after another. According to yesterday's news reports, the Japanese army suddenly launched a two-pronged attack on Rehe, one from Yizhou and the other from Chaoyang Temple, using armored vehicles as the vanguard and fiercely attacking Nanling Pass. They also dispatched seven planes to drop bombs, destroying all the buildings. I ask, what should the military and political authorities do?

Although Dong’s Rehe army is resisting desperately, the lower-ranking officers are furious and enraged, and they telegraph Tang Yulin, urging him to issue a resistance order quickly. However, Tang has made no response. How can Dong's army alone resist for long? They will inevitably be sacrificed under Japanese bombs and artillery fire, and the map of Rehe will change color. I ask, what to do? It is also reported that the Japanese plan to occupy Rehe and then sign a treaty with Puyi to cede the three provinces to Japan, while at the same time coveting Beijing and Tianjin, supporting the restoration of the Qing dynasty under Xuantong. Geographically speaking, if Rehe is lost, Beijing and Tianjin will not be easy to defend. Then, the Manchu restorationists will once again enter the pass with great fanfare and stage their signature act of the "Emperor Dream." I ask, what to do? Since they have dreamed of becoming emperors and establishing their small court in the Northeast, they will certainly not be satisfied with that. They will inevitably, under the banner of the Japanese, be ambitious and press forward step by step. The Japanese, of course, will use these brainless puppets to open up new territories one after another. I ask, what to do?

Seeing that the authorities have no solution and the military is irresponsible, the people either "flee north to the barbarians or flee south to Guangdong." They either call themselves slaves, present court tablets, and willingly become third- or fourth-class slaves, or they run under the banner of red and do the work of mercilessly killing people. I ask, what to do?

Correction: In yesterday's commentary, the title "To Contributors" was mistakenly printed as "Report." This correction is made.

Science

The Light Bulb 188

— Shen Yong

With the advancement of science, how fortunate people are to have gained control over nature. Since the invention of the light bulb, haven't we conquered the terrifying darkness? Now, the application of light bulbs is very common. In places like Shanghai, almost every household uses them. At night, the main roads are illuminated as bright as day. But we must know how much blood and sweat the inventor spent and how much time it took. Therefore, we cannot help but study it.

Before understanding its structure, we should first know its principle. Originally, when an electric current passes through a metal with high resistance, it generates heat, and when the heat reaches a very high temperature, it emits light.

Therefore, a light bulb is a glass sphere with a very thin metal filament inside. When an electric current passes through it, this metal filament emits light. According to the above principle, this metal filament must have three conditions:

First, it must have great resistance, so metals with resistance such as platinum must be used, and it must be very thin.

Second, it must be a metal that will not melt when exposed to high temperatures. Third, it must be a metal that will not vaporize.

Because this light-emitting filament caused many difficulties, it could only be resolved by various methods, so gradually there came about the perfect result we have today. It can be divided into four periods, and now I will briefly explain them separately, so that you can understand its structure.

(1) Platinum Period: During this period, a glass bulb was not used. Instead, two copper pillars were used, with a very thin platinum wire (the filament) connecting the two ends. Then, the electric current was passed through, and the platinum wire emitted light, becoming the earliest electric lamp. But this was very dangerous, because without a cover, it was easy to catch fire. So the second step was to cover the light-emitting platinum wire with a glass cover, using very thick platinum strips to connect the filament, with the two ends exposed outside the cover, in order to conduct electricity. If we still used this kind of light bulb today, made of expensive platinum, it would not only be impossible to make it widespread, but even the very wealthy would probably not dare to use it. So, soon it progressed to the second period.

(2) Carbon Filament Period: Using carbon filament instead of platinum certainly made it much cheaper, but there were two prerequisite difficulties: first, how to make the carbon into thin filaments; second, how to prevent the carbon filaments from vaporizing. It took a lot of time and research to find the answers. The solution to the first problem was to split bamboo into thin filaments, and after a long time of sunning and baking, when it became very dry, to immerse it in concentrated sulfuric acid, and it would become carbon filaments. What about solving the second problem? The air inside the glass bulb had to be completely extracted, so that it became a vacuum, and then it would not vaporize. At this time, it was finally successful, but after a short period of testing, it was still not satisfactory. Originally, the carbon filament was too brittle and could not be bent, so the inventor continued his research, and soon he reached the third period.

(3) Tungsten Period: At this time, tungsten wire was used to make the filament. Originally, the nature of tungsten was powder and could not be condensed. During the European War, a great German scientist invented a method of condensation. American scientist Edison, who was researching light bulbs, cooperated with him and made the tungsten into a filament. At this time, the two ends of the conductor exposed outside the bulb were still platinum. Now a cheaper metal (Invae) is also used. Therefore, the light bulb has become perfect and its value is very low and its utility is very common. The inventors who created happiness for the world are still not satisfied, because tungsten wire is easy to evaporate, and there is often a layer of black mist on the bulb, and it cannot be used for a long time, so they continue to work hard and reach the fourth period.

(4) Nitrogen Period: At this time, the glass bulb is filled with nitrogen, which on the one hand prevents the evaporation of tungsten wire, and on the other hand saves the difficult procedure of extracting a vacuum. Since then, we have the cheap, durable and beautiful light bulb that we use today.

From the above, we can see how much effort the scientists put in to create a small light bulb. And there are so many treasures in the world waiting for people to discover and create all kinds of things for people to use. We really want to learn from Edison to discover treasures and create happiness for mankind!

Society Improvement Discussion Group

My Views on Improving General Social Psychology 189

— Fan Shizhi

Perhaps everyone thinks this way: the current society, especially Chinese society, is bad, deformed, semi-feudal, and unhealthy. It is still in a transitional period where the old society has not completely collapsed and the new society has not been completely built. Only people in this transitional era are often the most painful and depressed, as if wandering at a crossroads, not knowing where to go. Therefore, they feel dissatisfied with this reality, express disapproval, and feel that the distance to the ideal society cannot be measured.

Therefore, the "Society Improvement Discussion Group" in this column was born in response to the needs of the times. However, most of the previous discussions focused on material aspects or the improvement of the external environment, and there was little discussion on the improvement of the general psychology of each individual. It must be known that society itself will not be riddled with diseases and become unmanageable. Therefore, what makes it riddled with diseases and unmanageable is still gradually created by each individual who makes up this society. And the reason why each individual creates this kind of bad society is still because there is a deeply rooted and unbreakable remnant (that is, psychology) in their minds that is enough to hinder social progress and prevent the birth of a new society, lurking and active, causing the skeleton of the old society to raise its head again, the remnants of the old society to continue to grow, the construction of the new society to have no way to start, and the spirit of the new society to have no way to realize.

The worst of these psychologies include the following:

(1) Selfishness

(2) Hypocrisy and deception

(3) Emphasis on appearance

(4) Suspicion and conspiracy

With a selfish psychology, one cannot be selfless, honest, and law-abiding. With a hypocritical and deceptive psychology, one cannot be calm, responsible, and honest. With a psychology that emphasizes appearance, one cannot be down-to-earth and realistic. With a psychology of suspicion and conspiracy, one cannot trust each other and unite. If we want the society and the country to embark on a bright and smooth road, we must thoroughly eradicate these four kinds of poisons left over from the old society, and we must thoroughly improve these four kinds of bad psychologies left over from the old society.

Sacrifice Spirit

Tuberculosis Patient 190

— I

When her husband left her sickbed, her bean-sized tears fell like raindrops, her face turned from pale to gray, and she buried her head in the quilt, her thin shoulders twitching constantly. This moved all the patients in the third-class ward and surprised them greatly: "Why is she so sad?" "Miss Li?!" Huang Qiuying, who was sleeping next to her, asked earnestly, "Why are you so sad? Didn't the doctor say that your illness requires special rest?"

She was still crying, and crying even more pitifully. After a long time, she turned her face and sobbed to Huang Qiuying; "I can't escape this sea of suffering, my illness can't be cured, I hope I can die sooner, at this time I feel that death has great significance for me."

At this time, she had no tears and no more crying, only this desperate, low voice. However, the compassionate Huang Qiuying still comforted her softly;

"But you can't think like that, illnesses can always be cured, as long as you can rest well. In fact, everyone will die, but no one wants to die, because death is ultimately very scary."

"But, I feel that death is very happy for me." After that, she spoke even more eloquently; "You know, the doctor has proved that my tuberculosis is more serious than before. Four months ago, I stayed here for a while. When the doctor allowed me to go out to recuperate, my friends said that I was much healthier than when I entered the hospital. Of course, I needed better rest. But we young people are always easily excited, and I simply cannot get used to a quiet life. Since the outbreak of the Shanghai war, I have firmly joined the nursing team because everyone should bear the responsibility of anti-imperialism. Needless to say, I was very busy at that time, and I even had very little sleep. As a result, my temperature increased, from 37 degrees to 39 or 40 degrees. Of course, my illness relapsed, and sometimes I even coughed up blood. :: Friend! Do you think that a person who can't work like this is simply a waste? From that time on, I felt that my existence was really too meaningless."

"Don't say it anymore, rest for a while now, you're talking too much." Huang Qiuying was very worried about her and now dissuaded her. However, she did not stop talking because of her dissuasion, she continued to speak, and her tone was so desolate and plaintive.

"My friend, although we only have two or three months of friendship, I believe in you very much, I feel that you are my true sympathizer, so I boldly want to ask you for help. There is still a child in my family who is less than two years old, and I love him very much. After I die, I hope you can often go to see him, and care for him as you care for your own children. If there is really a soul after death, then my soul will be comforted by your love! Friend, this is my last request."

"But why do you have to say that? Didn't you say that your husband loves you and your child very much?"

"No, my good friend, you know that my husband just came to say goodbye to me. He has joined the XX Suicide Squad, and he will leave tonight, I think we will not have a chance to meet again, because he is going to fight in close quarters, fighting for the survival of the nation, and I am in such a critical condition. But, my husband! I hope to see him one last time before I die! I want to have such a good opportunity."

She was crying again.

Finally, she said decisively;

"But, friend! You must not tell him my unfortunate news when he is killing the enemy, because he loves me too much, and he may abandon his great responsibility because of this!"

After that, she stopped talking, looking straight ahead, completely immersed in deep fantasy.

Pessimism

Autumn Wind, Autumn Rain, Sadden People to Death 191

— Yi Ping

"Cry, I cried, the nameless sorrow that had been abandoned for a long time gently struck my heart again; the first wave of dark shadows that were difficult to eliminate was as uncomfortable as suffocating, the inexplicable grief, I cried for a long time, and now my heart seems to be much relieved::

A melancholy young man, which could be seen from his thin cheeks and dull eyes, he bit the other end of the pen, watching a small tree swaying in the wind and rain outside the window,

"Poor little tree, you symbolize my destiny," his mouth moved slightly, and a tear that had been held back in his eye socket finally rolled down,

"Since" he shook his head, as if trying to dispel all the pain, and continued to write his diary, "my younger siblings were unreasonably made to suffer by his mother, although they were born of a different mother, I love them as much as life, because I am already a completely soulless walking corpse, they - my father's flesh and blood - I must make them continue my father's legacy, in their weak hearts, how can I keep this kind of bad image, so I resolutely embarked on my drifting journey, the ends of the earth, stay anywhere, maintain the happiness of my whole family, over the years, my father's spirit in heaven followed me like this, I struggled, I struggled, and when I felt a little discouraged, my father appeared in front of me again, and the life of drifting also had a special flavor and was full of interest, this time the war gave me a major blow, the lives and property of the Chinese people, the government completely has no ability to protect, a small family that I have been struggling to manage for several years has been buried in the fire, although this little thing is not worth anyone's attention, it is a great loss to me in my whole life, I escaped from the fire, am I not ridiculed for being greedy for life and afraid of death? But what is the use of the posthumous glory of dying on the battlefield? I can eat, fight, struggle::

Suddenly a desolate and desperate singing voice came from the two alleys, he knew it was an old man and his granddaughter, swaying in the autumn wind and rain, this intermittent singing voice made people unbearable to listen to, he pushed away the diary, jumped onto the bed, buried his head in the pillow, and cried out loud again the poor little tree was broken in the waist by the autumn wind and rain, and leaned obliquely in the mud and water by the roadside.

Zhu Dingjin is fined twenty yuan for possessing opium. The number of days detained before the verdict will be deducted from the fine at a rate of one day for two yuan. The number of days detained before the verdict will be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one. Shanghai Local Court 195

Criminal Judgment: Gu Xu Shi and others regarding the opium case. Gu Xu Shi is fined fifty yuan for possessing opium paraphernalia with the intention of using it for criminal purposes. Imprisonment days

can be offset against the fine at a rate of two days for one yuan. Wang Ziming is sentenced to one month of imprisonment and fined twenty yuan for smoking opium. Imprisonment days can be offset against the sentence at a rate of two days for one day. Zhu Ximing regarding the theft case. Zhu Ximing is sentenced to thirty days of detention for theft. Imprisonment days can be offset against the detention at a rate of two days for one day. Zhang A'er regarding the theft case. Zhang A'er is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for breaking and entering to commit theft at night. Imprisonment days can be offset against the sentence at a rate of two days for one day. Shen Zhaolin and others regarding the case of disrupting a family. Tao Zhaolin is sentenced to one year of imprisonment for luring a girl under the age of twenty away from her guardian with the intention of making a profit. Imprisonment days can be offset against the sentence at a rate of two days for one day. Shen Xiaoshan's trial is suspended. Li Da regarding the theft case. Li Da is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for committing theft at the train station. Imprisonment days can be offset against the sentence at a rate of two days for one day. Zhu Dongbao regarding the assault case. Zhu Dongbao is fined ten yuan for causing bodily harm to another person. Imprisonment days can be offset against the fine at a rate of two days for one yuan, and he must also pay a total of thirty yuan for medical expenses to Hu Xingtai and Hu Cao Shi. Wang Ranji and others accuse Jin Huaihua and others of obstructing freedom and destruction of property. This private prosecution is not accepted. Zhang Shiqing and others regarding the theft case. Zhang Shiqing is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for breaking into a residence at night to commit theft with three or more people. Imprisonment days can be offset against the sentence at a rate of two days for one day. Trial for Zhang Qingji and Xiao Binglang is partially suspended. Quan Huiqing, also known as Quan Gan-ting, and others regarding the case of fraud, assault, opium, and false accusation. Quan Huiqing, also known as Quan Gan-ting, is sentenced to one year of imprisonment and fined sixty yuan for providing a building for others to smoke opium with the intention of making a profit. He is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for the crime of false accusation. He is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for the crime of fraud. He is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for causing bodily harm to another person. The combined sentence is one year and two months of imprisonment and a fine of sixty yuan. Imprisonment days can be offset against the sentence at a rate of two days for one day. Wang Fuxing is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined thirty yuan for helping to provide a building for others to smoke opium with the intention of making a profit. Imprisonment days can be offset against the sentence at a rate of two days for one day. Mao Guangcai regarding the assault case. This public prosecution is not accepted. Tang Jinfu regarding the assault case. This public prosecution is not accepted. Wang Changgen accuses Xue Debao of theft. This private prosecution is not accepted. Fan Shi regarding the assault case. Fan Shi is sentenced to twenty days of detention for causing bodily harm to another person. Imprisonment days can be offset against the detention at a rate of two days for one day.

Civil Judgment: Hechangcheng Customs Broker vs. Kangxie Gonghang, Dong Sun Shiyuan, et al., over debt. The defendants Kangxie Gonghang, Dong Sun Shiyuan, Sun Shenliang, and Li Fucai shall be jointly and severally liable for repaying the plaintiff silver one thousand five hundred ninety-five taels, six mace, and nine fen, plus interest at an annual rate of five percent from the date of filing the lawsuit until the date of execution. If they are unable to repay, Liang Dongsheng of Longjihao Dong should be held liable for the payment. Xu Yunqing should also be responsible for a proportional share of the repayment. The defendants Sun Shiyuan, Sun Shenliang, and Li Fucai bear the litigation costs jointly and severally. Bao Ruman vs. Lu Yongxing Store Owner, et al., over bean payment. The defendant Tang Liankui shall repay the plaintiff goods payment of two hundred eighty-two yuan and seven jiao in foreign currency. The Lu Yongxing Store Owner shall repay the plaintiff goods payment of ninety yuan in foreign currency. The defendants shall bear the litigation costs proportionally. Xu Boquan vs. Shen Enjian over debt. The defendant shall pay the plaintiff silver one hundred thirty-seven taels and nine mace and eight fen, of which seventy-seven taels and nine mace and eight fen shall accrue legal late payment interest at an annual rate of five percent from June 13, 21, and sixty taels shall accrue legal late payment interest at an annual rate of five percent from July 4 of the same year, both until the date of execution. The plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected. The plaintiff bears fifteen percent of the litigation costs, and the defendant bears fourteen of fifteen percent. Chen Atang vs. Zhenhe Factory over debt. Hechang Iron Factory's debt of one hundred twenty yuan in rent to the plaintiff shall be the responsibility of the defendant to pay on behalf of. The defendant bears the litigation costs. The defendant shall repay the plaintiff silver one hundred five yuan and return the section of land on Zhongxing Road to the plaintiff. The defendant bears the litigation costs. Gu Baoxiang vs. Xinxin Xieji Printing Company over bill payment. The defendant shall pay the plaintiff bill payment of fifty yuan in foreign currency. The defendant bears the litigation costs. Ding Deng Lihua vs. Qian Meiqin over mortgage payment. The defendant shall repay the plaintiff silver forty thousand taels, plus agreed-upon interest calculated at a monthly rate of nine percent from the date of the loan until the date of execution. The defendant bears the litigation costs. Zhang Zhiqing vs. Wang Lunbo, et al., over divorce and alimony. The defendant Wang Lunbo shall divorce the plaintiff and pay alimony and damages of one thousand yuan in silver dollars. The plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected. The defendant Wang Lunbo bears seven-tenths of the litigation costs, and the plaintiff bears three-tenths.

It is understood from the petition that there is no reliable evidence that the aforementioned Li Han Shi stole silver dollars, and it is not appropriate to issue a summons based solely on one statement. You are hereby notified. Lu Qingde petitions for legal action. It is understood from the petition that you must come to court to be questioned before a decision can be made. Sha Huaqing accuses Wang Caiming of financial fraud. It is understood from the petition that there is no procedure for filing a criminal case. The request is denied. (Above dates: August 20)
